		}

ai_will_do = { modifier = { factor = 0 afr_is_tribal = yes  date < 1875.1.1 } modifier = { factor = 0 num_of_naval_factories < 1 }

				factor = 1.5
				num_of_naval_factories > 5
			}
		}
	}
